  if n==1<br />

  end<br />
  return s..C(a)..S..C(b)..s..p..f(n-2,N)..s..C(c)..S..C(d)..s..p<br />

    <td align="left">@DrGreenEggsandIronMan not really anymore. It's kinda like a really golfy markup language. Basically there are different modes of operation (specified by the first byte) that manipulate the code and the input. Then if the result starts with a backtick, it chops off the backtick and the next mode and starts again with either everything after an exclamation point in the code,a new line from stdin or the last input if stdin is exhausted for input. It's kinda a bit like Slashes, actually.</td>
